<pr_description>
No VM metrics with Centos/RHEL for Openstack
### Kepler Version

0.10.0 or later (Current/Supported)

### Bug Description

On Openstack for exemple, the virtual machine hypervisor is provided by install qem-kvm:
```
qemu-kvm-core-17:8.2.0-11.el9_4.14.x86_64 : qemu-kvm core components                                                           
Repo        : rhosp-rhel-9.4-appstream
Matched from:                      
Filename    : /usr/libexec/qemu-kvm
```
Then the usage is like: 
`/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm -name guest=instance-0000008b,debug-threads=on -S -object {"qom-type":"secret","id":"masterKey0","format":"raw","file":"/var/lib/libvirt/qemu/domain-25-instance-0000008b/master-key.aes"} -machine pc-q35-rhel9.4.0,usb=off,dump-guest-core=off,hpet=off,acpi=on -accel kvm -cpu Broadwell-IBRS [...] `

So of course, because Kepler is only looking for: 
https://github.com/sustainable-computing-io/kepler/blob/0339f536e97ec74a3813fa784bd5f4d489d75891/internal/resource/vm.go#L15

then it can't work...

### Steps to Reproduce

RHEL/CentOS: yum install qemu-kvm-core

### Expected Behavior

kepler_vm_* metrics are present with the right information of the VM. 

### Environment

Any Centos / RHEL

### Logs and Error Messages

```shell

```

### Additional Context

_No response_

     1	// SPDX-FileCopyrightText: 2025 The Kepler Authors
     2	// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0
     3	
     4	package resource
     5	
     6	import (
     7	        "fmt"
     8	        "path/filepath"
     9	        "regexp"
    10	        "strings"
    11	)
    12	
    13	var (
    14	        // QEMU/KVM patterns
    15	        qemuPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`bin/qemu-system-\w+`)
    16	
    17	        // TODO: add patterns for virtual box,  VMware, Xen
    18	
    19	        // VM process name patterns
    20	        vmProcessPatterns = map[*regexp.Regexp]Hypervisor{
    21	                qemuPattern: KVMHypervisor,
    22	        }
    23	)
    24	
    25	// vmInfoFromProc detects if a process is a VM process and extracts VM info
    26	func vmInfoFromProc(proc procInfo) (*VirtualMachine, error) {
    27	        // Check command line for VM processes
    28	        cmdline, err := proc.CmdLine()
    29	        if err != nil {
    30	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to get process cmdline: %w", err)
    31	        }
    32	
    33	        if len(cmdline) == 0 {
    34	                return nil, nil
    35	        }
    36	
    37	        hypervisor, vmID := vmInfoFromCmdLine(cmdline)
    38	        if hypervisor == UnknownHypervisor {
    39	                return nil, nil
    40	        }
    41	
    42	        vm := &VirtualMachine{
    43	                ID:         vmID,
    44	                Hypervisor: hypervisor,
    45	        }
    46	
    47	        // Try to get VM name from command line arguments
    48	        vm.Name = vmNameFromCmdLine(cmdline, hypervisor)
    49	
    50	        if vm.Name == "" {
    51	                vm.Name = fmt.Sprintf("%s-%s", hypervisor, vmID[:8])
    52	        }
    53	
    54	        return vm, nil
    55	}
    56	
    57	// vmInfoFromCmdLine extracts VM information from command line
    58	func vmInfoFromCmdLine(cmdline []string) (Hypervisor, string) {
    59	        if len(cmdline) == 0 {
    60	                return UnknownHypervisor, ""
    61	        }
    62	        exe := filepath.Base(cmdline[0])
    63	        fullCmd := strings.Join(cmdline, " ")
    64	
    65	        for pattern, hypervisor := range vmProcessPatterns {
    66	                if pattern.MatchString(exe) || pattern.MatchString(fullCmd) {
    67	                        vmID := extractVMID(cmdline, hypervisor)
    68	
    69	                        // If VM ID is still empty, make one up from the command line parameter hash
    70	                        // TODO: validate if this this is a good idea
    71	                        if vmID == "" {
    72	                                vmID = generateVMID(fullCmd)
    73	                        }
    74	                        return hypervisor, vmID
    75	                }
    76	        }
    77	
    78	        return UnknownHypervisor, ""
    79	}
    80	
    81	// extractVMID extracts VM ID from command line arguments based on hypervisor
    82	func extractVMID(cmdline []string, hypervisor Hypervisor) string {
    83	        switch hypervisor {
    84	        case KVMHypervisor:
    85	                return extractQemuMachineID(cmdline)
    86	        default:
    87	                return ""
    88	        }
    89	}
    90	
    91	// extractQemuMachineID extracts VM ID from QEMU/KVM command line arguments, if present
    92	// otherwise returns the VM name
    93	func extractQemuMachineID(cmdline []string) string {
    94	        for i, arg := range cmdline {
    95	                if arg == "-uuid" && i+1 < len(cmdline) {
    96	                        return cmdline[i+1]
    97	                }
    98	        }
    99	        return qemuVMNameFromCmdLine(cmdline)
   100	}
   101	
   102	// generateVMID generates a VM ID when one can't be extracted
   103	func generateVMID(fullCmd string) string {
   104	        hash := fmt.Sprintf("%x", []byte(fullCmd))
   105	        if len(hash) > 16 {
   106	                return hash[:16]
   107	        }
   108	        return hash
   109	}
   110	
   111	// vmNameFromCmdLine extracts VM name from command line arguments
   112	func vmNameFromCmdLine(cmdline []string, hypervisor Hypervisor) string {
   113	        switch hypervisor {
   114	        case KVMHypervisor:
   115	                return qemuVMNameFromCmdLine(cmdline)
   116	        default:
   117	                return ""
   118	        }
   119	}
   120	
   121	// qemuVMNameFromCmdLine extracts VM name from QEMU command line
   122	func qemuVMNameFromCmdLine(cmdline []string) string {
   123	        for i, arg := range cmdline {
   124	                if arg == "-name" && i+1 < len(cmdline) {
   125	                        value := cmdline[i+1]
   126	                        // QEMU -name can have format "guest=name,debug-threads=on"
   127	                        if strings.Contains(value, "guest=") {
   128	                                parts := strings.Split(value, ",")
   129	
   130	                                for _, part := range parts {
   131	                                        if strings.HasPrefix(part, "guest=") {
   132	                                                return strings.TrimPrefix(part, "guest=")
   133	                                        }
   134	                                }
   135	                        }
   136	                        return value
   137	                }
   138	
   139	                if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "-name=") {
   140	                        return strings.TrimPrefix(arg, "-name=")
   141	                }
   142	        }
   143	        return ""
   144	}
   145

Now I can see the issue. The pattern on line 15 is:
```go
qemuPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`bin/qemu-system-\w+`)
```

This only matches executables that contain `bin/qemu-system-*` in their path. However, on RHEL/CentOS systems with qemu-kvm-core, the executable is `/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm`, which doesn't match this pattern.

   300	                expected:     expect{nil, true},
   301	        }, {

   303	                cmdline:  []string{},

   305	        }}

   336	func TestVMClone(t *testing.T) {
   337	        t.Run("Full VM clone", func(t *testing.T) {
   338	                original := &VirtualMachine{
   339	                        ID:           "df12672f-fedb-4f6f-9d51-0166868835fb",
   340	                        Name:         "test-vm",
   341	                        Hypervisor:   KVMHypervisor,
   342	                        CPUTimeDelta: 123.45,
   343	                }
   344	
   345	                clone := original.Clone()
   346	
   347	                // Check that the clone has the same values
   348	                assert.Equal(t, original.ID, clone.ID)
   349	                assert.Equal(t, original.Name, clone.Name)
   350	                assert.Equal(t, original.Hypervisor, clone.Hypervisor)
   351	                assert.Equal(t, float64(0), clone.CPUTimeDelta) // CPUTime shouldn't be cloned
   352	        })
   353	
   354	        t.Run("Clone nil VM", func(t *testing.T) {
   355	                var nilVM *VirtualMachine
   356	                nilClone := nilVM.Clone()
   357	                assert.Nil(t, nilClone, "Cloning nil VM should return nil")
   358	        })
   359	}

     4	package resource
     5	
     6	type ProcessType string
     7	
     8	const (
     9	        UnknownProcess   ProcessType = ""
    10	        RegularProcess   ProcessType = "regular"
    11	        ContainerProcess ProcessType = "container"
    12	        VMProcess        ProcessType = "vm"
    13	)
    14	
    15	type Process struct {
    16	        // static
    17	        PID  int
    18	        Comm string
    19	        Exe  string
    20	        Type ProcessType
    21	
    22	        Container      *Container
    23	        VirtualMachine *VirtualMachine
    24	
    25	        // Dynamic
    26	        CPUTotalTime float64 // total cpu time used by the process
    27	        CPUTimeDelta float64 // cpu time used by the process since last refresh
    28	}
    29	
    30	// Container represents metadata about a container
    31	type Container struct {
    32	        ID      string
    33	        Name    string
    34	        Runtime ContainerRuntime
    35	
    36	        Pod *Pod
    37	
    38	        // Resource usage tracking
    39	        CPUTotalTime float64 // total cpu time used by the container so far
    40	        CPUTimeDelta float64 // cpu time used by the container since last refresh
    41	}
    42	
    43	type ContainerRuntime string
    44	
    45	const (
    46	        UnknownRuntime    ContainerRuntime = "unknown"
    47	        DockerRuntime     ContainerRuntime = "docker"
    48	        ContainerDRuntime ContainerRuntime = "containerd"
    49	        CrioRuntime       ContainerRuntime = "crio"
    50	        PodmanRuntime     ContainerRuntime = "podman"
    51	        KubePodsRuntime   ContainerRuntime = "kubernetes"
    52	)
    53	
    54	// Clone creates a deep copy of a Container
    55	func (c *Container) Clone() *Container {
    56	        if c == nil {
    57	                return nil
    58	        }
    59	
    60	        clone := &Container{
    61	                ID:      c.ID,
    62	                Name:    c.Name,
    63	                Runtime: c.Runtime,
    64	        }
    65	
    66	        return clone
    67	}
    68	
    69	// VirtualMachine represents metadata about a virtual machine
    70	type VirtualMachine struct {
    71	        ID         string
    72	        Name       string
    73	        Hypervisor Hypervisor
    74	
    75	        // Resource usage tracking
    76	        CPUTotalTime float64 // total cpu time used by the VM so far
    77	        CPUTimeDelta float64 // cpu time used by the VM since last refresh
    78	}
    79	
    80	type Hypervisor string
    81	
    82	const (
    83	        UnknownHypervisor Hypervisor = "unknown"
    84	
    85	        KVMHypervisor Hypervisor = "kvm"
    86	
    87	        // TODO: add patterns for these hypervisors
    88	        VirtualBoxHypervisor Hypervisor = "virtualbox"
    89	        VMwareHypervisor     Hypervisor = "vmware"
    90	        XenHypervisor        Hypervisor = "xen"
    91	)
    92	
    93	// Clone creates a deep copy of a VirtualMachine
    94	func (vm *VirtualMachine) Clone() *VirtualMachine {
    95	        if vm == nil {
    96	                return nil
    97	        }
    98	
    99	        return &VirtualMachine{
   100	                ID:         vm.ID,
   101	                Name:       vm.Name,
   102	                Hypervisor: vm.Hypervisor,
   103	        }
   104	}
   105	
   106	type Pod struct {
   107	        ID        string
   108	        Name      string
   109	        Namespace string
   110	
   111	        // Resource usage tracking
   112	        CPUTotalTime float64 // total cpu time used by the Pod so far
   113	        CPUTimeDelta float64 // cpu time used by the Pod since last refresh
   114	}
   115	
   116	func (p *Pod) Clone() *Pod {
   117	        if p == nil {
   118	                return nil
   119	        }
   120	        return &Pod{
   121	                ID:        p.ID,
   122	                Name:      p.Name,
   123	                Namespace: p.Namespace,
   124	        }
   125	}
   126

"""
Test script to demonstrate the RHEL/CentOS qemu-kvm issue.
This script will run the Go tests with additional test cases for qemu-kvm.
"""

import subprocess
import sys

# Test cases to add
test_cases = """
The issue is that on RHEL/CentOS, the QEMU executable path is:
/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm

But the current pattern only matches:
bin/qemu-system-\\w+

So commands like:
/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm -name guest=instance-0000008b,debug-threads=on -S -object {...} -machine pc-q35-rhel9.4.0 ...

Will NOT be detected as VM processes.
"""

def run_go_test():
    """Run the Go tests for VM detection"""
    print("Running Go tests for VM detection...")
    result = subprocess.run(
        ["go", "test", "-v", "./internal/resource", "-run", "TestVMInfoFromCmdLine"],
        cwd="/testbed",
        capture_output=True,
        text=True
    )
    print(result.stdout)
    print(result.stderr)
    return result.returncode == 0

def test_pattern_matching():
    """Test if the current pattern matches RHEL qemu-kvm"""
    print("\n" + "="*80)
    print("Testing pattern matching...")
    print("="*80)
    
    # Create a simple Go test program
    test_program = """
package main

import (
    "fmt"
    "regexp"
)

func main() {
    // Current pattern
    qemuPattern := regexp.MustCompile(`bin/qemu-system-\\w+`)
    
    testCases := []struct {
        name string
        path string
    }{
        {"Ubuntu/Debian QEMU", "/usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64"},
        {"RHEL/CentOS qemu-kvm", "/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm"},
    }
    
    fmt.Println("Testing current pattern: bin/qemu-system-\\\\w+")
    fmt.Println()
    
    for _, tc := range testCases {
        matches := qemuPattern.MatchString(tc.path)
        fmt.Printf("%-30s %-40s -> %v\\n", tc.name, tc.path, matches)
    }
}
"""
    
    # Write and run the test program
    with open("/tmp/test_pattern.go", "w") as f:
        f.write(test_program)
    
    result = subprocess.run(
        ["go", "run", "/tmp/test_pattern.go"],
        capture_output=True,
        text=True
    )
    print(result.stdout)
    if result.stderr:
        print("STDERR:", result.stderr)
    
    return "false" in result.stdout.lower()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    print(test_cases)
    print()
    
    # Test pattern matching
    has_issue = test_pattern_matching()
    
    if has_issue:
        print("\n" + "="*80)
        print("ISSUE CONFIRMED: /usr/libexec/qemu-kvm is NOT matched by current pattern")
        print("="*80)

    print("Running existing Go tests...")
    print("="*80)

    if tests_pass:
        print("\nExisting tests PASS")
    else:
        print("\nExisting tests FAIL")
    
    sys.exit(0 if (has_issue and tests_pass) else 1)

cd /testbed && cat > /tmp/test_qemu_kvm.go << 'EOF'
package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"path/filepath"
	"regexp"
	"strings"
)

var (
	// Current pattern (from the code)
	qemuPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`bin/qemu-system-\w+`)
)

func testCurrentPattern(cmdline []string) bool {
	if len(cmdline) == 0 {
		return false
	}
	exe := filepath.Base(cmdline[0])
	fullCmd := strings.Join(cmdline, " ")

	return qemuPattern.MatchString(exe) || qemuPattern.MatchString(fullCmd)
}

func main() {
	testCases := []struct {
		name    string
		cmdline []string
		expect  bool
	}{
		{
			name: "Ubuntu/Debian QEMU x86_64",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64",
				"-name", "guest=test-vm",
			},
			expect: true,
		},
		{
			name: "RHEL/CentOS qemu-kvm",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm",
				"-name", "guest=instance-0000008b,debug-threads=on",
				"-S",
				"-machine", "pc-q35-rhel9.4.0",
			},
			expect: true, // Should match but currently doesn't
		},
	}

	fmt.Println("Testing current QEMU pattern: bin/qemu-system-\\w+")
	fmt.Println(strings.Repeat("=", 80))

	allPass := true
	for _, tc := range testCases {
		result := testCurrentPattern(tc.cmdline)
		status := "✅ PASS"
		if result != tc.expect {
			status = "❌ FAIL"
			allPass = false
		}
		fmt.Printf("%s: %s (expected: %v, got: %v)\n", status, tc.name, tc.expect, result)
	}

	fmt.Println(strings.Repeat("=", 80))
	if !allPass {
		fmt.Println("\n⚠️  Current pattern does NOT support RHEL/CentOS qemu-kvm!")
	} else {
		fmt.Println("\n✅ All tests pass!")
	}
}
EOF

The simplest fix is to update the pattern to match both:
- `bin/qemu-system-\w+` (original)
- `qemu-kvm` (new for RHEL/CentOS)

Let me create a better pattern. Since it checks both the basename and the full command, we can use: `(bin/qemu-system-\w+|qemu-kvm)`

Actually, looking at the code more carefully:
- Line 62: `exe := filepath.Base(cmdline[0])` - this gets the basename like `qemu-system-x86_64` or `qemu-kvm`
- Line 66: It matches against both `exe` and `fullCmd`

So for the basename `qemu-kvm`, the pattern needs to match just `qemu-kvm`. For the full path `/usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64`, the pattern `bin/qemu-system-\w+` matches.

The best pattern would be: `(bin/qemu-system-\w+|qemu-kvm)`

cat > /tmp/test_fixed_pattern.go << 'EOF'
package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"path/filepath"
	"regexp"
	"strings"
)

var (
	// Updated pattern (from the fix)
	qemuPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`(bin/qemu-system-\w+|qemu-kvm)`)
)

func testPattern(cmdline []string) bool {
	if len(cmdline) == 0 {
		return false
	}
	exe := filepath.Base(cmdline[0])
	fullCmd := strings.Join(cmdline, " ")

	return qemuPattern.MatchString(exe) || qemuPattern.MatchString(fullCmd)
}

func main() {
	testCases := []struct {
		name    string
		cmdline []string
		expect  bool
	}{
		{
			name: "Ubuntu/Debian QEMU x86_64",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64",
				"-name", "guest=test-vm",
			},
			expect: true,
		},
		{
			name: "Ubuntu/Debian QEMU aarch64",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/bin/qemu-system-aarch64",
				"-name", "guest=arm-vm",
			},
			expect: true,
		},
		{
			name: "RHEL/CentOS qemu-kvm",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm",
				"-name", "guest=instance-0000008b,debug-threads=on",
				"-S",
				"-machine", "pc-q35-rhel9.4.0",
			},
			expect: true,
		},
		{
			name: "Not a VM process",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/bin/firefox",
			},
			expect: false,
		},
	}

	fmt.Println("Testing UPDATED QEMU pattern: (bin/qemu-system-\\w+|qemu-kvm)")
	fmt.Println(strings.Repeat("=", 80))

	allPass := true
	for _, tc := range testCases {
		result := testPattern(tc.cmdline)
		status := "✅ PASS"
		if result != tc.expect {
			status = "❌ FAIL"
			allPass = false
		}
		fmt.Printf("%s: %s (expected: %v, got: %v)\n", status, tc.name, tc.expect, result)
	}

	fmt.Println(strings.Repeat("=", 80))
	if !allPass {
		fmt.Println("\n❌ Some tests failed!")
	} else {
		fmt.Println("\n✅ All tests pass!")
	}
}
EOF

The test file hasn't changed. Let me verify our fix more thoroughly by creating a comprehensive test that simulates the exact command from the PR:

🎬 ACTION
cat > /tmp/test_rhel_fix.go << 'EOF'
package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"regexp"
	"strings"
)

var (
	// Updated pattern (from the fix)
	qemuPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`(bin/qemu-system-\w+|qemu-kvm)`)
)

func vmInfoFromCmdLine(cmdline []string) (string, string) {
	if len(cmdline) == 0 {
		return "unknown", ""
	}
	exe := filepath.Base(cmdline[0])
	fullCmd := strings.Join(cmdline, " ")

	if qemuPattern.MatchString(exe) || qemuPattern.MatchString(fullCmd) {
		// Extract VM name
		for i, arg := range cmdline {
			if arg == "-name" && i+1 < len(cmdline) {
				value := cmdline[i+1]
				if strings.Contains(value, "guest=") {
					parts := strings.Split(value, ",")
					for _, part := range parts {
						if strings.HasPrefix(part, "guest=") {
							return "kvm", strings.TrimPrefix(part, "guest=")
						}
					}
				}
				return "kvm", value
			}
		}
		return "kvm", "unnamed-vm"
	}

	return "unknown", ""
}

func main() {
	testCases := []struct {
		name         string
		cmdline      []string
		expectHV     string
		expectVMName string
	}{
		{
			name: "RHEL/CentOS qemu-kvm (from PR description)",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm",
				"-name", "guest=instance-0000008b,debug-threads=on",
				"-S",
				"-object", `{"qom-type":"secret","id":"masterKey0","format":"raw","file":"/var/lib/libvirt/qemu/domain-25-instance-0000008b/master-key.aes"}`,
				"-machine", "pc-q35-rhel9.4.0,usb=off,dump-guest-core=off,hpet=off,acpi=on",
				"-accel", "kvm",
				"-cpu", "Broadwell-IBRS",
			},
			expectHV:     "kvm",
			expectVMName: "instance-0000008b",
		},
		{
			name: "Ubuntu/Debian qemu-system-x86_64",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64",
				"-name", "guest=ubuntu-vm,debug-threads=on",
				"-uuid", "df12672f-fedb-4f6f-9d51-0166868835fb",
			},
			expectHV:     "kvm",
			expectVMName: "ubuntu-vm",
		},
		{
			name: "Not a VM",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/bin/firefox",
				"--profile", "/home/user/.mozilla",
			},
			expectHV:     "unknown",
			expectVMName: "",
		},
	}

	allPass := true
	fmt.Println("Testing RHEL/CentOS qemu-kvm Support")
	fmt.Println(strings.Repeat("=", 80))

	for _, tc := range testCases {
		hv, vmName := vmInfoFromCmdLine(tc.cmdline)
		
		hvMatch := hv == tc.expectHV
		nameMatch := vmName == tc.expectVMName
		
		status := "✅ PASS"
		if !hvMatch || !nameMatch {
			status = "❌ FAIL"
			allPass = false
		}
		
		fmt.Printf("\n%s: %s\n", status, tc.name)
		fmt.Printf("  Expected: hypervisor=%s, vmName=%s\n", tc.expectHV, tc.expectVMName)
		fmt.Printf("  Got:      hypervisor=%s, vmName=%s\n", hv, vmName)
	}

	fmt.Println(strings.Repeat("=", 80))
	if !allPass {
		fmt.Println("\n❌ Some tests failed!")
		os.Exit(1)
	} else {
		fmt.Println("\n✅ All tests pass! RHEL/CentOS qemu-kvm is now supported!")
	}
}
EOF
go run /tmp/test_rhel_fix.go

cat > /tmp/final_test.go << 'EOF'
package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"regexp"
	"strings"
)

var (
	// Updated pattern (from the fix)
	qemuPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`(bin/qemu-system-\w+|qemu-kvm)`)
)

func testPattern(cmdline []string) bool {
	if len(cmdline) == 0 {
		return false
	}
	exe := filepath.Base(cmdline[0])
	fullCmd := strings.Join(cmdline, " ")

	return qemuPattern.MatchString(exe) || qemuPattern.MatchString(fullCmd)
}

func main() {
	testCases := []struct {
		name    string
		cmdline []string
		expect  bool
	}{
		{
			name: "RHEL/CentOS qemu-kvm (libexec path)",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm",
				"-name", "guest=instance-0000008b",
			},
			expect: true,
		},
		{
			name: "RHEL/CentOS qemu-kvm (different libexec path)",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/opt/libexec/qemu-kvm",
				"-name", "guest=test-vm",
			},
			expect: true,
		},
		{
			name: "Ubuntu/Debian qemu-system-x86_64",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64",
				"-name", "guest=ubuntu-vm",
			},
			expect: true,
		},
		{
			name: "Ubuntu/Debian qemu-system-aarch64",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/bin/qemu-system-aarch64",
				"-name", "guest=arm-vm",
			},
			expect: true,
		},
		{
			name: "Ubuntu/Debian qemu-system-ppc64",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/bin/qemu-system-ppc64",
				"-name", "guest=ppc-vm",
			},
			expect: true,
		},
		{
			name: "Not a VM - firefox",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/bin/firefox",
			},
			expect: false,
		},
		{
			name: "Not a VM - similar name but not qemu",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/bin/my-qemu-kvm-monitor",
			},
			expect: false,
		},
		{
			name: "Edge case - qemu-kvm in path",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/custom/path/to/qemu-kvm",
				"-m", "2048",
			},
			expect: true,
		},
	}

	fmt.Println("Final comprehensive test for QEMU/KVM pattern fix")
	fmt.Println(strings.Repeat("=", 80))

	allPass := true
	for _, tc := range testCases {
		result := testPattern(tc.cmdline)
		status := "✅ PASS"
		if result != tc.expect {
			status = "❌ FAIL"
			allPass = false
		}
		fmt.Printf("%s: %s\n", status, tc.name)
		if result != tc.expect {
			fmt.Printf("  Expected: %v, Got: %v\n", tc.expect, result)
		}
	}

	fmt.Println(strings.Repeat("=", 80))
	if !allPass {
		fmt.Println("\n❌ Some tests failed!")
		os.Exit(1)
	} else {
		fmt.Println("\n✅ All tests pass! RHEL/CentOS qemu-kvm support verified!")
	}
}
EOF

cat > /tmp/final_test_qemu.go << 'EOF'
package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"regexp"
	"strings"
)

var (
	// Updated pattern (from the fix)
	qemuPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`(bin/qemu-system-\w+|qemu-kvm)`)
)

func testPattern(cmdline []string) bool {
	if len(cmdline) == 0 {
		return false
	}
	exe := filepath.Base(cmdline[0])
	fullCmd := strings.Join(cmdline, " ")

	return qemuPattern.MatchString(exe) || qemuPattern.MatchString(fullCmd)
}

func main() {
	testCases := []struct {
		name    string
		cmdline []string
		expect  bool
	}{
		{
			name: "RHEL/CentOS qemu-kvm (libexec path)",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm",
				"-name", "guest=instance-0000008b",
			},
			expect: true,
		},
		{
			name: "RHEL/CentOS qemu-kvm (different libexec path)",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/opt/libexec/qemu-kvm",
				"-name", "guest=test-vm",
			},
			expect: true,
		},
		{
			name: "Ubuntu/Debian qemu-system-x86_64",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64",
				"-name", "guest=ubuntu-vm",
			},
			expect: true,
		},
		{
			name: "Ubuntu/Debian qemu-system-aarch64",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/bin/qemu-system-aarch64",
				"-name", "guest=arm-vm",
			},
			expect: true,
		},
		{
			name: "Ubuntu/Debian qemu-system-ppc64",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/bin/qemu-system-ppc64",
				"-name", "guest=ppc-vm",
			},
			expect: true,
		},
		{
			name: "Not a VM - firefox",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/bin/firefox",
			},
			expect: false,
		},
		{
			name: "Not a VM - similar name but not qemu",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/bin/my-qemu-kvm-monitor",
			},
			expect: false,
		},
		{
			name: "Edge case - qemu-kvm in path",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/custom/path/to/qemu-kvm",
				"-m", "2048",
			},
			expect: true,
		},
	}

	fmt.Println("Final comprehensive test for QEMU/KVM pattern fix")
	fmt.Println(strings.Repeat("=", 80))

	allPass := true
	for _, tc := range testCases {
		result := testPattern(tc.cmdline)
		status := "✅ PASS"
		if result != tc.expect {
			status = "❌ FAIL"
			allPass = false
		}
		fmt.Printf("%s: %s\n", status, tc.name)
		if result != tc.expect {
			fmt.Printf("  Expected: %v, Got: %v\n", tc.expect, result)
		}
	}

	fmt.Println(strings.Repeat("=", 80))
	if !allPass {
		fmt.Println("\n❌ Some tests failed!")
		os.Exit(1)
	} else {
		fmt.Println("\n✅ All tests pass! RHEL/CentOS qemu-kvm support verified!")
	}
}
EOF

cat > /tmp/test_final_qemu.go << 'EOF'
package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"regexp"
	"strings"
)

var (
	// Updated pattern with exact match for qemu-kvm
	qemuPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`(bin/qemu-system-\w+|^qemu-kvm$)`)
)

func testPattern(cmdline []string) bool {
	if len(cmdline) == 0 {
		return false
	}
	exe := filepath.Base(cmdline[0])
	fullCmd := strings.Join(cmdline, " ")

	return qemuPattern.MatchString(exe) || qemuPattern.MatchString(fullCmd)
}

func main() {
	testCases := []struct {
		name    string
		cmdline []string
		expect  bool
	}{
		{
			name: "RHEL/CentOS qemu-kvm (libexec path)",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm",
				"-name", "guest=instance-0000008b",
			},
			expect: true,
		},
		{
			name: "Ubuntu/Debian qemu-system-x86_64",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64",
				"-name", "guest=ubuntu-vm",
			},
			expect: true,
		},
		{
			name: "Not a VM - similar name but not qemu",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/bin/my-qemu-kvm-monitor",
			},
			expect: false,
		},
		{
			name: "Edge case - qemu-kvm in path",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/custom/path/to/qemu-kvm",
				"-m", "2048",
			},
			expect: true,
		},
	}

	fmt.Println("Testing final QEMU/KVM pattern: (bin/qemu-system-\\w+|^qemu-kvm$)")
	fmt.Println(strings.Repeat("=", 80))

	allPass := true
	for _, tc := range testCases {
		result := testPattern(tc.cmdline)
		status := "✅ PASS"
		if result != tc.expect {
			status = "❌ FAIL"
			allPass = false
		}
		fmt.Printf("%s: %s\n", status, tc.name)
		if result != tc.expect {
			fmt.Printf("  Expected: %v, Got: %v\n", tc.expect, result)
		}
	}

	fmt.Println(strings.Repeat("=", 80))
	if !allPass {
		fmt.Println("\n❌ Some tests failed!")
		os.Exit(1)
	} else {
		fmt.Println("\n✅ All tests pass!")
	}
}
EOF

+"/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm",
+"-name", "guest=instance-0000008b,debug-threads=on",
+"-S",
+"-object", `{"qom-type":"secret","id":"masterKey0","format":"raw","file":"/var/lib/libvirt/qemu/domain-25-instance-0000008b/master-key.aes"}`,
+"-machine", "pc-q35-rhel9.4.0,usb=off,dump-guest-core=off,hpet=off,acpi=on",
+"-accel", "kvm",
+"-cpu", "Broadwell-IBRS",
+}
+
+// This should be detected as KVM but currently isn't
+hypervisor, vmID := resource.TestVMInfoFromCmdLine(cmdline)
+
+fmt.Printf("Hypervisor: %s\n", hypervisor)
+fmt.Printf("VM ID: %s\n", vmID)
+
+if hypervisor == "unknown" {
+fmt.Println("\n❌ FAILED: RHEL/CentOS qemu-kvm not detected!")
+return
+}
+
+if hypervisor == "kvm" {
+fmt.Println("\n✅ SUCCESS: RHEL/CentOS qemu-kvm detected correctly!")
+}
+}

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""
+Test script to demonstrate the RHEL/CentOS qemu-kvm issue.
+This script will run the Go tests with additional test cases for qemu-kvm.
+"""
+
+import subprocess
+import sys
+
+# Test cases to add
+test_cases = """
+The issue is that on RHEL/CentOS, the QEMU executable path is:
+/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm
+
+But the current pattern only matches:
+bin/qemu-system-\\w+
+
+So commands like:
+/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm -name guest=instance-0000008b,debug-threads=on -S -object {...} -machine pc-q35-rhel9.4.0 ...
+
+Will NOT be detected as VM processes.
+"""
+
+def run_go_test():
+    """Run the Go tests for VM detection"""
+    print("Running Go tests for VM detection...")
+    result = subprocess.run(
+        ["go", "test", "-v", "./internal/resource", "-run", "TestVMInfoFromCmdLine"],
+        cwd="/testbed",
+        capture_output=True,
+        text=True
+    )
+    print(result.stdout)
+    print(result.stderr)
+    return result.returncode == 0
+
+def test_pattern_matching():
+    """Test if the current pattern matches RHEL qemu-kvm"""
+    print("\n" + "="*80)
+    print("Testing pattern matching...")
+    print("="*80)
+    
+    # Create a simple Go test program
+    test_program = """
+package main
+
+import (
+    "fmt"
+    "regexp"
+)
+
+func main() {
+    // Current pattern
+    qemuPattern := regexp.MustCompile(`bin/qemu-system-\\w+`)
+    
+    testCases := []struct {
+        name string
+        path string
+    }{
+        {"Ubuntu/Debian QEMU", "/usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64"},
+        {"RHEL/CentOS qemu-kvm", "/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm"},
+    }
+    
+    fmt.Println("Testing current pattern: bin/qemu-system-\\\\w+")
+    fmt.Println()
+    
+    for _, tc := range testCases {
+        matches := qemuPattern.MatchString(tc.path)
+        fmt.Printf("%-30s %-40s -> %v\\n", tc.name, tc.path, matches)
+    }
+}
+"""
+    
+    # Write and run the test program
+    with open("/tmp/test_pattern.go", "w") as f:
+        f.write(test_program)
+    
+    result = subprocess.run(
+        ["go", "run", "/tmp/test_pattern.go"],
+        capture_output=True,
+        text=True
+    )
+    print(result.stdout)
+    if result.stderr:
+        print("STDERR:", result.stderr)
+    
+    return "false" in result.stdout.lower()
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    print(test_cases)
+    print()
+    
+    # Test pattern matching
+    has_issue = test_pattern_matching()
+    
+    if has_issue:
+        print("\n" + "="*80)
+        print("ISSUE CONFIRMED: /usr/libexec/qemu-kvm is NOT matched by current pattern")
+        print("="*80)
+    
+    # Run existing tests
+    print("\n" + "="*80)
+    print("Running existing Go tests...")
+    print("="*80)
+    tests_pass = run_go_test()
+    
+    if tests_pass:
+        print("\nExisting tests PASS")
+    else:
+        print("\nExisting tests FAIL")
+    
+    sys.exit(0 if (has_issue and tests_pass) else 1)

</diff>

// SPDX-FileCopyrightText: 2025 The Kepler Authors
// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

package resource

import (
	"fmt"
	"path/filepath"
	"regexp"
	"strings"
)

var (
	// QEMU/KVM patterns
	qemuPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`bin/qemu-system-\w+`)

	// TODO: add patterns for virtual box,  VMware, Xen

	// VM process name patterns
	vmProcessPatterns = map[*regexp.Regexp]Hypervisor{
		qemuPattern: KVMHypervisor,
	}
)

// vmInfoFromProc detects if a process is a VM process and extracts VM info
func vmInfoFromProc(proc procInfo) (*VirtualMachine, error) {
	// Check command line for VM processes
	cmdline, err := proc.CmdLine()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to get process cmdline: %w", err)

with open('/testbed/internal/resource/vm.go', 'r') as f:
    lines = f.readlines()

# Find and replace the qemuPattern line
new_lines = []
for i, line in enumerate(lines):
    if 'qemuPattern = regexp.MustCompile' in line and 'bin/qemu-system' in line:
        # Add comment lines before
        new_lines.append('\t// Matches:\n')
        new_lines.append('\t// - /usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64 (Ubuntu/Debian)\n')
        new_lines.append('\t// - /usr/bin/qemu-system-aarch64 (Ubuntu/Debian ARM)\n')
        new_lines.append('\t// - /usr/libexec/qemu-kvm (RHEL/CentOS)\n')
        # Replace pattern
        new_lines.append('\tqemuPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`(bin/qemu-system-\\w+|^qemu-kvm$)`)\n')
    else:
        new_lines.append(line)

with open('/testbed/internal/resource/vm.go', 'w') as f:
    f.writelines(new_lines)

print("Fixed!")
PYEOF

 // qemuVMNameFromCmdLine extracts VM name from QEMU command line
 func qemuVMNameFromCmdLine(cmdline []string) string {
-	for i, arg := range cmdline {
-		if arg == "-name" && i+1 < len(cmdline) {
-			value := cmdline[i+1]
-			// QEMU -name can have format "guest=name,debug-threads=on"
-			if strings.Contains(value, "guest=") {
-				parts := strings.Split(value, ",")
-
-				for _, part := range parts {
-					if strings.HasPrefix(part, "guest=") {
-						return strings.TrimPrefix(part, "guest=")
-					}
-				}
-			}

-	}

+        for i, arg := range cmdline {
+                if arg == "-name" && i+1 < len(cmdline) {
+                        value := cmdline[i+1]
+                        // QEMU -name can have format "guest=name,debug-threads=on"
+                        if strings.Contains(value, "guest=") {
+                                parts := strings.Split(value, ",")
+
+                                for _, part := range parts {
+                                        if strings.HasPrefix(part, "guest=") {
+                                                return strings.TrimPrefix(part, "guest=")
+                                        }
+                                }
+                        }
+                        return value
+                }
+
+                if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "-name=") {
+                        return strings.TrimPrefix(arg, "-name=")
+                }
+        }
+        return ""
 }
